static void Frame3102_Thread6056_Pass5 (const VApp &app)
{
	{
	VkClearValue  clearValues[1u] = {};
	VkRenderPassBeginInfo  renderPassBeginInfo = {};
	renderPassBeginInfo.pNext = null;
	renderPassBeginInfo.sType = VK_STRUCTURE_TYPE_RENDER_PASS_BEGIN_INFO;
	// current clear value depends of render pass
	// .depthStencil = { 1.000000f, 53u }
	// .color.uint32 = { 1065353216u, 53u, 0u, 0u }
	clearValues[0u].color = { 1.000000f, 0.000000f, 0.000000f, 0.000000f };
	renderPassBeginInfo.renderPass = app.GetResource(RenderPassID(16ull));
